          <script type="text/javascript">
           /*设置域名列表*/
		  	function initDomainList(){
		      	var domainData = window.domainDataList;
		      	if(domainData){

			        var defaultSelect = domainData['defaultSelect'];
			        var defaultSelectType = domainData.suffix_detail_list[defaultSelect]['suffix_type'] || 'en';

			        var suffixListHtml = [];
			        for(var index in domainData.suffix_list){
			          	var domainSuffix = domainData.suffix_list[index];
			          	var suffixDetail = domainData.suffix_detail_list[domainSuffix];

			          	suffixListHtml.push('<li class="J_suffixItem" type="'+suffixDetail['suffix_type']+'">.'+domainSuffix+'</li>');
			        }
		        	$('.J_suffixList ul').html(suffixListHtml.join(''));
					$('.J_iptDomain').keydown(function(event){
						if(event.keyCode==13){ 
							event.preventDefault();
							$('.J_btnSubmitSchDomain').click();  
						}
					});
              		$('.J_suffixItem').on('click', function(event) {
						event.preventDefault();
						var tp = $(this).attr('type');
						var ds = $(this).html();
						$('.J_selectedSuffix').replaceWith('<span type="'+ tp +'" class="name J_selectedSuffix">'+ ds +'</span>');
						$('.J_suffixBox').removeClass('suf-expanded');
              		});
		      	}
		    }
          </script>

         (function(){

    // 判断是否访问终端
    function osFilter() {  
        var ua = navigator.userAgent,  
        isWindowsPhone = /(?:Windows Phone)/.test(ua),  
        isSymbian = /(?:SymbianOS)/.test(ua) || isWindowsPhone,   
        isAndroid = /(?:Android)/.test(ua),   
        isFireFox = /(?:Firefox)/.test(ua),   
        isChrome = /(?:Chrome|CriOS)/.test(ua),  
        isTablet = /(?:iPad|PlayBook)/.test(ua) || (isAndroid && !/(?:Mobile)/.test(ua)) || (isFireFox && /(?:Tablet)/.test(ua)),  
        isPhone = /(?:iPhone)/.test(ua) && !isTablet,  
        isPc = !isPhone && !isAndroid && !isSymbian;  
        return {  
              isTablet: isTablet,  
              isPhone: isPhone,  
              isAndroid : isAndroid,  
              isPc : isPc  
        };  
    }; 
    var linkH5 = "//domain.aliyun.com/domain/index.htm";
    var linkPc = "";
    var searchParam = window.location.search;
    // 在tms页面，不跳转
    var host = window.location.host;
    var os = osFilter();
    if(linkH5){
      linkH5 = searchParam ? linkH5 + searchParam : linkH5;
      if(!os.isPc || os.isTablet) {
        window.location = linkH5; 
      }
    } else if(linkPc && host !== 'tms.alibaba-inc.com') {
      linkPc = searchParam ? linkPc + searchParam : linkPc;
      if(os.isPc) {
        window.location = linkPc;
      }
    } 
  })();
